The study finds that AI washing significantly suppresses farmers' digital financial behavior; the higher the degree of AI washing, the lower the response level of farmers' digital financial behavior. Moreover, AI washing indirectly inhibits farmers' behavioral responses by exacerbating knowledge exclusion and risk exclusion. Social capital can positively moderate the negative impact of AI washing; among farmer groups with high social capital, the suppressive effect of AI washing on digital financial behavior is significantly weaker than that among groups with low social capital. In response, this paper suggests that regulatory authorities establish a strict information disclosure system for AI technology, conduct differentiated digital financial education to enhance the identification capabilities of vulnerable groups, promote digital financial mutual aid groups to leverage the protective effects of social capital, improve the consumer protection mechanism for farmers in digital finance, and set up pilot "Digital Inclusive Finance Demonstration Counties," etc.

摘要：在數位金融快速發展的背景下，一些金融科技公司出現了「AI 洗牌」的現象，即它們誇大自己的 AI 能力，同時對實際的 AI 資源投資不足。本文基於 CHFS2019 數據和 15-20 家金融科技公司的 AI 投資數據構建了一個企業級 AI 洗牌指數，分析並測試其對農民數位金融行為反應的影響。研究發現，AI 洗牌顯著抑制了農民的數位金融行為；AI 洗牌的程度越高，農民的數位金融行為反應水平越低。此外，AI 洗牌通過加劇知識排斥和風險排斥間接抑制農民的行為反應。社會資本可以正向調節 AI 洗牌的負面影響；在社會資本高的農民群體中，AI 洗牌對數位金融行為的抑制效應顯著弱於社會資本低的群體。針對這一點，本文建議監管機構建立嚴格的 AI 技術信息披露制度，進行差異化的數位金融教育以增強弱勢群體的識別能力，促進數位金融互助組織以發揮社會資本的保護效應，改善農民在數位金融中的消費者保護機制，並設立試點「數位包容性金融示範縣」等。

##### **From Weak Cues to Real Identities: Evaluating Inference-Driven De-Anonymization in LLM Agents**
2603.18382v1 by Myeongseob Ko, Jihyun Jeong, Sumiran Singh Thakur, Gyuhak Kim, Ruoxi Jia

Anonymization is widely treated as a practical safeguard because re-identifying anonymous records was historically costly, requiring domain expertise, tailored algorithms, and manual corroboration. We study a growing privacy risk that may weaken this barrier: LLM-based agents can autonomously reconstruct real-world identities from scattered, individually non-identifying cues. By combining these sparse cues with public information, agents resolve identities without bespoke engineering. We formalize this threat as \emph{inference-driven linkage} and systematically evaluate it across three settings: classical linkage scenarios (Netflix and AOL), \emph{InferLink} (a controlled benchmark varying task intent, shared cues, and attacker knowledge), and modern text-rich artifacts. Without task-specific heuristics, agents successfully execute both fixed-pool matching and open-ended identity resolution. In the Netflix Prize setting, an agent reconstructs 79.2\% of identities, significantly outperforming a 56.0\% classical baseline. Furthermore, linkage emerges not only under explicit adversarial prompts but also as a byproduct of benign cross-source analysis in \emph{InferLink} and unstructured research narratives. These findings establish that identity inference -- not merely explicit information disclosure -- must be treated as a first-class privacy risk; evaluations must measure what identities an agent can infer.

摘要：匿名化被廣泛視為一種實用的保護措施，因為重新識別匿名記錄在歷史上是昂貴的，需依賴領域專業知識、量身定制的算法和人工驗證。<lb/>我們研究了一個日益增長的隱私風險，這可能削弱這一障礙：基於LLM的代理可以自主從分散的、單獨不具識別性的線索中重建現實世界的身份。<lb/>通過將這些稀疏的線索與公共信息結合，代理能夠在沒有定制工程的情況下解決身份問題。<lb/>我們將這一威脅形式化為\emph{推理驅動的連結}，並在三個場景中系統性地評估它：經典連結場景（Netflix和AOL）、\emph{InferLink}（一個受控基準，變化任務意圖、共享線索和攻擊者知識）以及現代文本豐富的文獻。<lb/>在沒有特定任務啟發式的情況下，代理成功執行了固定池匹配和開放式身份解析。<lb/>在Netflix獎項設定中，一個代理重建了79.2\%的身份，顯著超過56.0\%的經典基準。<lb/>此外，連結不僅在明確的對抗性提示下出現，還作為\emph{InferLink}和非結構化研究敘述中良性跨源分析的副產品出現。<lb/>這些發現確立了身份推理——而不僅僅是明確的信息披露——必須被視為一級隱私風險；評估必須衡量代理可以推斷出哪些身份。

##### **PlanTwin: Privacy-Preserving Planning Abstractions for Cloud-Assisted LLM Agents**
2603.18377v2 by Guangsheng Yu, Qin Wang, Rui Lang, Shuai Su, Xu Wang

Cloud-hosted large language models (LLMs) have become the de facto planners in agentic systems, coordinating tools and guiding execution over local environments. In many deployments, however, the environment being planned over is private, containing source code, files, credentials, and metadata that cannot be exposed to the cloud. Existing solutions address adjacent concerns, such as execution isolation, access control, or confidential inference, but they do not control what cloud planners observe during planning: within the permitted scope, \textit{raw environment state is still exposed}.
  We introduce PlanTwin, a privacy-preserving architecture for cloud-assisted planning without exposing raw local context. The key idea is to project the real environment into a \textit{planning-oriented digital twin}: a schema-constrained and de-identified abstract graph that preserves planning-relevant structure while removing reconstructable details. The cloud planner operates solely on this sanitized twin through a bounded capability interface, while a local gatekeeper enforces safety policies and cumulative disclosure budgets. We further formalize the privacy-utility trade-off as a capability granularity problem, define architectural privacy goals using $(k,δ)$-anonymity and $ε$-unlinkability, and mitigate compositional leakage through multi-turn disclosure control.
  We implement PlanTwin as middleware between local agents and cloud planners and evaluate it on 60 agentic tasks across ten domains with four cloud planners. PlanTwin achieves full sensitive-item non-disclosure (SND = 1.0) while maintaining planning quality close to full-context systems: three of four planners achieve PQS $> 0.79$, and the full pipeline incurs less than 2.2\% utility loss.

摘要：雲端托管的大型語言模型（LLMs）已成為代理系統中的事實上規劃者，協調工具並指導在本地環境中的執行。然後，在許多部署中，所規劃的環境是私有的，包含源代碼、文件、憑證和無法暴露於雲端的元數據。現有的解決方案解決了相鄰的問題，例如執行隔離、訪問控制或機密推理，但它們並不控制雲端規劃者在規劃過程中觀察到的內容：在允許的範圍內，\textit{原始環境狀態仍然被暴露}。

我們介紹了PlanTwin，一種隱私保護架構，用於雲輔助規劃而不暴露原始本地上下文。關鍵思想是將真實環境投影到\textit{以規劃為導向的數位雙胞胎}：一個結構受限且去識別化的抽象圖，保留與規劃相關的結構，同時去除可重建的細節。雲端規劃者僅通過一個有限能力介面在這個經過清理的雙胞胎上運作，而本地守門人則執行安全政策和累積披露預算。我們進一步將隱私-效用權衡形式化為能力粒度問題，使用$(k,δ)$-匿名性和$ε$-不可連結性定義架構隱私目標，並通過多輪披露控制來減輕組合泄漏。

我們將PlanTwin實現為本地代理和雲端規劃者之間的中介，並在十個領域的60個代理任務上進行評估，使用四個雲端規劃者。PlanTwin實現了完全的敏感項目非披露（SND = 1.0），同時保持接近全上下文系統的規劃質量：四個規劃者中有三個達到PQS $&gt; 0.79$，而整個管道的效用損失少於2.2\%。

##### **Interpretability without actionability: mechanistic methods cannot correct language model errors despite near-perfect internal representations**
2603.18353v1 by Sanjay Basu, Sadiq Y. Patel, Parth Sheth, Bhairavi Muralidharan, Namrata Elamaran, Aakriti Kinra, John Morgan, Rajaie Batniji

Language models encode task-relevant knowledge in internal representations that far exceeds their output performance, but whether mechanistic interpretability methods can bridge this knowledge-action gap has not been systematically tested. We compared four mechanistic interpretability methods -- concept bottleneck steering (Steerling-8B), sparse autoencoder feature steering, logit lens with activation patching, and linear probing with truthfulness separator vector steering (Qwen 2.5 7B Instruct) -- for correcting false-negative triage errors using 400 physician-adjudicated clinical vignettes (144 hazards, 256 benign). Linear probes discriminated hazardous from benign cases with 98.2% AUROC, yet the model's output sensitivity was only 45.1%, a 53-percentage-point knowledge-action gap. Concept bottleneck steering corrected 20% of missed hazards but disrupted 53% of correct detections, indistinguishable from random perturbation (p=0.84). SAE feature steering produced zero effect despite 3,695 significant features. TSV steering at high strength corrected 24% of missed hazards while disrupting 6% of correct detections, but left 76% of errors uncorrected. Current mechanistic interpretability methods cannot reliably translate internal knowledge into corrected outputs, with implications for AI safety frameworks that assume interpretability enables effective error correction.

摘要：語言模型在內部表示中編碼與任務相關的知識，這些知識遠超過它們的輸出性能，但機械解釋方法是否能彌合這一知識與行動之間的差距尚未經過系統性測試。我們比較了四種機械解釋方法——概念瓶頸引導（Steerling-8B）、稀疏自編碼器特徵引導、帶有激活修補的邏輯透鏡，以及使用真實性分隔向量引導的線性探測（Qwen 2.5 7B Instruct）——以糾正使用400個醫生裁定的臨床小插曲（144個危險、256個良性）的假陰性分流錯誤。線性探測以98.2%的AUROC區分危險與良性案例，但模型的輸出靈敏度僅為45.1%，知識與行動之間存在53個百分點的差距。概念瓶頸引導糾正了20%的漏檢危險，但擾亂了53%的正確檢測，與隨機擾動無法區分（p=0.84）。儘管有3,695個顯著特徵，SAE特徵引導產生了零效果。高強度的TSV引導糾正了24%的漏檢危險，同時擾亂了6%的正確檢測，但仍有76%的錯誤未被糾正。目前的機械解釋方法無法可靠地將內部知識轉化為糾正的輸出，這對假設可解釋性能夠有效糾正錯誤的AI安全框架有重要影響。

##### **Approximate Subgraph Matching with Neural Graph Representations and Reinforcement Learning**
2603.18314v1 by Kaiyang Li, Shihao Ji, Zhipeng Cai, Wei Li

Approximate subgraph matching (ASM) is a task that determines the approximate presence of a given query graph in a large target graph. Being an NP-hard problem, ASM is critical in graph analysis with a myriad of applications ranging from database systems and network science to biochemistry and privacy. Existing techniques often employ heuristic search strategies, which cannot fully utilize the graph information, leading to sub-optimal solutions. This paper proposes a Reinforcement Learning based Approximate Subgraph Matching (RL-ASM) algorithm that exploits graph transformers to effectively extract graph representations and RL-based policies for ASM. Our model is built upon the branch-and-bound algorithm that selects one pair of nodes from the two input graphs at a time for potential matches. Instead of using heuristics, we exploit a Graph Transformer architecture to extract feature representations that encode the full graph information. To enhance the training of the RL policy, we use supervised signals to guide our agent in an imitation learning stage. Subsequently, the policy is fine-tuned with the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) that optimizes the accumulative long-term rewards over episodes. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our RL-ASM outperforms existing methods in terms of effectiveness and efficiency. Our source code is available at https://github.com/KaiyangLi1992/RL-ASM.

摘要：近似子圖匹配（ASM）是一項任務，旨在確定給定查詢圖在大型目標圖中的近似存在。作為一個 NP 困難問題，ASM 在圖分析中至關重要，應用範圍廣泛，從數據庫系統和網絡科學到生物化學和隱私。現有技術通常採用啟發式搜索策略，這無法充分利用圖信息，導致次優解。本文提出了一種基於強化學習的近似子圖匹配（RL-ASM）算法，利用圖變換器有效提取圖表示和基於 RL 的 ASM 策略。我們的模型基於分支限界算法，該算法一次從兩個輸入圖中選擇一對節點進行潛在匹配。我們不使用啟發式方法，而是利用圖變換器架構提取編碼完整圖信息的特徵表示。為了增強 RL 策略的訓練，我們使用監督信號來指導我們的代理進行模仿學習階段。隨後，該策略通過近端政策優化（PPO）進行微調，以優化整個回合的累積長期獎勵。在合成和真實世界數據集上的大量實驗表明，我們的 RL-ASM 在效果和效率方面優於現有方法。我們的源代碼可在 https://github.com/KaiyangLi1992/RL-ASM 獲得。

##### **Detection Is Cheap, Routing Is Learned: Why Refusal-Based Alignment Evaluation Fails**
2603.18280v1 by Gregory N. Frank

Current alignment evaluation mostly measures whether models encode dangerous concepts and whether they refuse harmful requests. Both miss the layer where alignment often operates: routing from concept detection to behavioral policy. We study political censorship in Chinese-origin language models as a natural experiment, using probes, surgical ablations, and behavioral tests across nine open-weight models from five labs. Three findings follow. First, probe accuracy alone is non-diagnostic: political probes, null controls, and permutation baselines can all reach 100%, so held-out category generalization is the informative test. Second, surgical ablation reveals lab-specific routing. Removing the political-sensitivity direction eliminates censorship and restores accurate factual output in most models tested, while one model confabulates because its architecture entangles factual knowledge with the censorship mechanism. Cross-model transfer fails, indicating that routing geometry is model- and lab-specific. Third, refusal is no longer the dominant censorship mechanism. Within one model family, hard refusal falls to zero while narrative steering rises to the maximum, making censorship invisible to refusal-only benchmarks. These results support a three-stage descriptive framework: detect, route, generate. Models often retain the relevant knowledge; alignment changes how that knowledge is expressed. Evaluations that audit only detection or refusal therefore miss the routing mechanism that most directly determines behavior.

摘要：目前的對齊評估主要衡量模型是否編碼危險概念以及是否拒絕有害請求。這兩者都忽略了對齊通常運作的層面：從概念檢測到行為政策的路由。我們將中國來源語言模型中的政治審查作為一個自然實驗進行研究，使用探針、外科切除和行為測試，涵蓋來自五個實驗室的九個開放權重模型。有三個發現。首先，僅僅依賴探針準確性並不能診斷：政治探針、無效對照和置換基準都可以達到100%，因此保留類別的泛化是有信息的測試。其次，外科切除揭示了實驗室特定的路由。去除政治敏感性方向消除了審查，並在大多數測試的模型中恢復了準確的事實輸出，而一個模型因其架構將事實知識與審查機制糾纏在一起而產生了虛構。跨模型轉移失敗，表明路由幾何是模型和實驗室特定的。第三，拒絕不再是主要的審查機制。在一個模型家族中，強硬拒絕降至零，而敘事引導則上升至最大，這使得審查對僅拒絕基準來說變得不可見。這些結果支持一個三階段的描述框架：檢測、路由、生成。模型通常保留相關知識；對齊改變了該知識的表達方式。因此，僅審計檢測或拒絕的評估會錯過最直接決定行為的路由機制。

##### **MolRGen: A Training and Evaluation Setting for De Novo Molecular Generation with Reasonning Models**
2603.18256v1 by Philippe Formont, Maxime Darrin, Ismail Ben Ayed, Pablo Piantanida

Recent advances in reasoning-based large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated substantial improvements in complex problem-solving tasks. Motivated by these advances, several works have explored the application of reasoning LLMs to drug discovery and molecular design. However, most existing approaches either focus on evaluation or rely on training setups that require ground-truth labels, such as molecule pairs with known property modifications. Such supervision is unavailable in \textit{de novo} molecular generation, where the objective is to generate novel molecules that optimize a desirability score without prior knowledge of high-scoring candidates. To bridge this gap, we introduce MolRGen, a large-scale benchmark and dataset for training and evaluating reasoning-based LLMs on \textit{de novo} molecular generation. Our contributions are threefold. First, we propose a setting to evaluate and train models for \textit{de novo} molecular generation and property prediction. Second, we introduce a novel diversity-aware top-$k$ score that captures both the quality and diversity of generated molecules. Third, we show our setting can be used to train LLMs for molecular generation, training a 24B LLM with reinforcement learning, and we provide a detailed analysis of its performance and limitations.

摘要：最近在基於推理的大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展顯示出在複雜問題解決任務中有顯著的改善。受到這些進展的激勵，幾項研究探索了將推理 LLM 應用於藥物發現和分子設計的可能性。然而，大多數現有的方法要麼專注於評估，要麼依賴於需要真實標籤的訓練設置，例如具有已知性質修改的分子對。在\textit{de novo} 分子生成中，這種監督是不可用的，因為其目標是生成新穎的分子，以優化一個期望分數，而不需要對高分候選者的先驗知識。為了填補這一空白，我們介紹了 MolRGen，一個用於訓練和評估基於推理的 LLM 在\textit{de novo} 分子生成上的大型基準和數據集。我們的貢獻有三個方面。首先，我們提出了一個設置來評估和訓練用於\textit{de novo} 分子生成和性質預測的模型。其次，我們引入了一種新穎的考慮多樣性的 top-$k$ 分數，該分數同時捕捉生成分子的質量和多樣性。第三，我們展示了我們的設置可以用於訓練 LLM 進行分子生成，並使用強化學習訓練了一個 24B 的 LLM，並提供了其性能和限制的詳細分析。

##### **How Psychological Learning Paradigms Shaped and Constrained Artificial Intelligence**
2603.18203v1 by Alex Anvi Eponon, Ildar Batyrshin, Christian E. Maldonado-Sifuentes, Grigori Sidorov

The dominant paradigms of artificial intelligence were shaped by learning theories from psychology: behaviorism inspired reinforcement learning, cognitivism gave rise to deep learning and memory-augmented architectures, and constructivism influenced curriculum learning and compositional approaches. This paper argues that each AI paradigm inherited not only the strengths but the structural limitations of the psychological theory that inspired it. Reinforcement learning cannot account for the internal structure of knowledge, deep learning compresses representations into opaque parameter spaces resistant to principled update, and current integrative approaches lack a formal account of how new understanding is constructed from existing components. The paper further examines a cross-cultural divergence in the interpretation of rote learning, arguing that the Eastern conception of memorization as a structured, multi-phase precursor to understanding offers an underexploited bridge between psychological theory and AI methodology. Drawing on the systematicity debate and critique of Aizawa of both classicism and connectionism, this paper introduces ReSynth, a trimodular framework that separates reasoning (Intellect), purpose (Identity), and knowledge (Memory) as architecturally independent components. The paper traces the genealogy from psychological paradigm to AI method, diagnoses the inherited limitations at each stage, and argues that adaptability, the central challenge of artificial general intelligence requires a representational architecture in which systematic behavior is a necessary consequence rather than an accidental property.

摘要：主流的人工智慧範式受到心理學學習理論的影響：行為主義啟發了強化學習，認知主義促成了深度學習和記憶增強架構，而建構主義則影響了課程學習和組合方法。本文主張，每個人工智慧範式不僅繼承了其啟發來源的心理學理論的優勢，還繼承了其結構性限制。強化學習無法解釋知識的內部結構，深度學習將表徵壓縮到不透明的參數空間，這些空間對原則性更新具有抵抗力，而當前的整合方法缺乏對如何從現有組件構建新理解的正式說明。本文進一步檢視了對死記硬背的跨文化解讀差異，主張東方對記憶的理解作為理解的結構性、多階段前驅，提供了一個未被充分利用的橋樑，將心理學理論與人工智慧方法論連結起來。本文借鑒了系統性辯論以及對經典主義和連結主義的相澤批評，介紹了ReSynth，一個三模組框架，將推理（智力）、目的（身份）和知識（記憶）作為建築上獨立的組件分開。本文追溯了從心理學範式到人工智慧方法的系譜，診斷了每個階段繼承的限制，並主張適應性，作為人工通用智慧的核心挑戰，需要一種表徵架構，其中系統性行為是必要的結果，而不是偶然的特性。

##### **Modeling the human lexicon under temperature variations: linguistic factors, diversity and typicality in LLM word associations**
2603.18171v1 by Maria Andueza Rodriguez, Marie Candito, Richard Huyghe

Large language models (LLMs) achieve impressive results in terms of fluency in text generation, yet the nature of their linguistic knowledge - in particular the human-likeness of their internal lexicon - remains uncertain. This study compares human and LLM-generated word associations to evaluate how accurately models capture human lexical patterns. Using English cue-response pairs from the SWOW dataset and newly generated associations from three LLMs (Mistral-7B, Llama-3.1-8B, and Qwen-2.5-32B) across multiple temperature settings, we examine (i) the influence of lexical factors such as word frequency and concreteness on cue-response pairs, and (ii) the variability and typicality of LLM responses compared to human responses. Results show that all models mirror human trends for frequency and concreteness but differ in response variability and typicality. Larger models such as Qwen tend to emulate a single "prototypical" human participant, generating highly typical but minimally variable responses, while smaller models such as Mistral and Llama produce more variable yet less typical responses. Temperature settings further influence this trade-off, with higher values increasing variability but decreasing typicality. These findings highlight both the similarities and differences between human and LLM lexicons, emphasizing the need to account for model size and temperature when probing LLM lexical representations.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在文本生成的流暢性方面取得了令人印象深刻的成果，但它們的語言知識的本質，尤其是其內部詞彙的類人特性，仍然不確定。這項研究比較了人類和LLM生成的詞彙聯想，以評估模型在多大程度上準確捕捉人類詞彙模式。利用來自SWOW數據集的英語提示-反應對和三個LLM（Mistral-7B、Llama-3.1-8B和Qwen-2.5-32B）在多個溫度設置下生成的新聯想，我們檢查了（i）詞彙因素如詞頻和具體性對提示-反應對的影響，以及（ii）LLM反應與人類反應相比的變異性和典型性。結果顯示，所有模型在頻率和具體性上都反映了人類的趨勢，但在反應的變異性和典型性上有所不同。像Qwen這樣的大型模型傾向於模仿單一的“原型”人類參與者，生成高度典型但變異性最小的反應，而像Mistral和Llama這樣的小型模型則產生更具變異性但不那麼典型的反應。溫度設置進一步影響這一權衡，較高的值增加了變異性但降低了典型性。這些發現突顯了人類和LLM詞彙之間的相似性和差異，強調在探討LLM詞彙表徵時需要考慮模型大小和溫度。

##### **TDAD: Test-Driven Agentic Development - Reducing Code Regressions in AI Coding Agents via Graph-Based Impact Analysis**
2603.17973v2 by Pepe Alonso, Sergio Yovine, Victor A. Braberman

AI coding agents can resolve real-world software issues, yet they frequently introduce regressions -- breaking tests that previously passed. Current benchmarks focus almost exclusively on resolution rate, leaving regression behavior under-studied. This paper presents TDAD (Test-Driven Agentic Development), an open-source tool that performs pre-change impact analysis for AI coding agents. TDAD builds a dependency map between source code and tests so that before committing a patch, the agent knows which tests to verify and can self-correct. The map is delivered as a lightweight agent skill -- a static text file the agent queries at runtime. Evaluated on SWE-bench Verified with two open-weight models running on consumer hardware (Qwen3-Coder 30B, 100 instances; Qwen3.5-35B-A3B, 25 instances), TDAD reduced regressions by 70% (6.08% to 1.82%) compared to a vanilla baseline. In contrast, adding TDD procedural instructions without targeted test context increased regressions to 9.94% -- worse than no intervention at all. When deployed as an agent skill with a different model and framework, TDAD improved issue-resolution rate from 24% to 32%, confirming that surfacing contextual information outperforms prescribing procedural workflows. All code, data, and logs are publicly available at https://github.com/pepealonso95/TDAD.

摘要：AI 編碼代理可以解決現實世界的軟體問題，但它們經常引入回歸——破壞之前通過的測試。當前的基準幾乎專注於解決率，導致回歸行為的研究不足。本文提出了 TDAD（測試驅動的代理開發），這是一個開源工具，用於對 AI 編碼代理進行變更前影響分析。TDAD 在源代碼和測試之間建立了依賴圖，以便在提交補丁之前，代理知道需要驗證哪些測試並能夠自我修正。該圖作為輕量級的代理技能交付——一個代理在運行時查詢的靜態文本文件。在 SWE-bench 上進行評估，使用兩個在消費者硬體上運行的開放權重模型（Qwen3-Coder 30B，100 個實例；Qwen3.5-35B-A3B，25 個實例），TDAD 將回歸率從 6.08% 降低到 1.82%，減少了 70%（相較於原始基準）。相比之下，添加 TDD 程序指令而不針對測試上下文的情況下，回歸率增加到 9.94%——甚至比沒有任何干預更糟。當作為代理技能與不同模型和框架部署時，TDAD 將問題解決率從 24% 提高到 32%，證實了呈現上下文信息的效果優於規定程序工作流程。所有代碼、數據和日誌都可以在 https://github.com/pepealonso95/TDAD 上公開獲取。

##### **CodeScout: An Effective Recipe for Reinforcement Learning of Code Search Agents**
2603.17829v1 by Lintang Sutawika, Aditya Bharat Soni, Bharath Sriraam R R, Apurva Gandhi, Taha Yassine, Sanidhya Vijayvargiya, Yuchen Li, Xuhui Zhou, Yilin Zhang, Leander Melroy Maben, Graham Neubig

A prerequisite for coding agents to perform tasks on large repositories is code localization - the identification of relevant files, classes, and functions to work on. While repository-level code localization has been performed using embedding-based retrieval approaches such as vector search, recent work has focused on developing agents to localize relevant code either as a standalone precursor to or interleaved with performing actual work. Most prior methods on agentic code search equip the agent with complex, specialized tools, such as repository graphs derived from static analysis. In this paper, we demonstrate that, with an effective reinforcement learning recipe, a coding agent equipped with nothing more than a standard Unix terminal can be trained to achieve strong results. Our experiments on three benchmarks (SWE-Bench Verified, Pro, and Lite) reveal that our models consistently achieve superior or competitive performance over 2-18x larger base and post-trained LLMs and sometimes approach performance provided by closed models like Claude Sonnet, even when using specialized scaffolds. Our work particularly focuses on techniques for re-purposing existing coding agent environments for code search, reward design, and RL optimization. We release the resulting model family, CodeScout, along with all our code and data for the community to build upon.

摘要：一個編碼代理在大型代碼庫上執行任務的前提是代碼定位——識別相關的文件、類別和函數以進行操作。雖然已經使用基於嵌入的檢索方法（例如向量搜索）進行了庫級代碼定位，但最近的研究集中在開發代理，以便將相關代碼定位為獨立的前驅或與實際工作交錯進行。大多數先前的代理代碼搜索方法為代理配備了複雜的專用工具，例如來自靜態分析的庫圖。本文中，我們展示了通過有效的強化學習配方，僅用標準Unix終端裝備的編碼代理可以被訓練以達到優異的結果。我們在三個基準（SWE-Bench Verified、Pro和Lite）上的實驗顯示，我們的模型在性能上始終優於或與2-18倍更大的基礎和後訓練LLM競爭，有時甚至接近像Claude Sonnet這樣的封閉模型提供的性能，即使在使用專用支架的情況下。我們的工作特別關注於重新利用現有編碼代理環境進行代碼搜索、獎勵設計和強化學習優化的技術。我們發布了結果模型系列CodeScout，以及我們的所有代碼和數據，供社區進一步構建。

##### **FailureMem: A Failure-Aware Multimodal Framework for Autonomous Software Repair**
2603.17826v1 by Ruize Ma, Yilei Jiang, Shilin Zhang, Zheng Ma, Yi Feng, Vincent Ng, Zhi Wang, Xiangyu Yue, Chuanyi Li, Lewei Lu

Multimodal Automated Program Repair (MAPR) extends traditional program repair by requiring models to jointly reason over source code, textual issue descriptions, and visual artifacts such as GUI screenshots. While recent LLM-based repair systems have shown promising results, existing approaches face several limitations: rigid workflow pipelines restrict exploration during debugging, visual reasoning is often performed over full-page screenshots without localized grounding, and failed repair attempts are rarely transformed into reusable knowledge. To address these challenges, we propose FailureMem, a multimodal repair framework that integrates three key mechanisms: a hybrid workflow-agent architecture that balances structured localization with flexible reasoning, active perception tools that enable region-level visual grounding, and a Failure Memory Bank that converts past repair attempts into reusable guidance. Experiments on SWE-bench Multimodal demonstrate FailureMem improves the resolved rate over GUIRepair by 3.7%.

摘要：多模態自動程式修復（MAPR）擴展了傳統的程式修復，要求模型共同推理源代碼、文本問題描述以及視覺物件，如 GUI 截圖。雖然最近基於 LLM 的修復系統顯示出有希望的結果，但現有的方法面臨幾個限制：僵化的工作流程管道限制了調試過程中的探索，視覺推理通常是在整個頁面的截圖上進行，而沒有局部的基礎，且失敗的修復嘗試很少轉化為可重用的知識。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了 FailureMem，一個多模態修復框架，整合了三個關鍵機制：一種混合工作流代理架構，平衡結構化定位與靈活推理，主動感知工具使得區域級別的視覺基礎成為可能，以及一個失敗記憶庫，將過去的修復嘗試轉化為可重用的指導。在 SWE-bench Multimodal 上的實驗表明，FailureMem 對 GUIRepair 的解決率提高了 3.7%。

##### **Intellectual Stewardship: Re-adapting Human Minds for Creative Knowledge Work in the Age of AI**
2603.18117v1 by Jianwei Zhang

Background: Amid the opportunities and risks introduced by generative AI, learning research needs to envision how human minds and responsibilities should re-adapt as AI continues to augment or automate various tasks.
  Approach: Drawing on theories of learning, intelligence, and knowledge creation, this conceptual paper proposes intellectual stewardship as a human-centered, conceptually grounded framework for advancing creative learning practices with AI.
  Key points: Students and teachers work as responsible governors of intellectual processes distributed across human and artificial systems, guided by five core principles. Being knowledge-wise involves understanding the evolving state of knowledge and taking purposeful actions to advance it. Being intelligence-wise emphasizes making informed choices about how to orchestrate distributed cognitive processes and resources. Being context-wise requires sensitivity to recognize opportunities and risks. Being ethics-wise foregrounds ethical judgment, responsibility, and care in the use of knowledge and intellectual power. Finally, self- and community-growing defines the overarching purpose, aligning intellectual work with personal development and the advancement of collective well-being.
  Contribution: The principles provide a lens for viewing the adaptation of human minds in AI-infused learning environments, calling for the development of meta-level dispositions and capabilities that characterize wisdom-oriented, socially responsible knowledge builders in the AI age.

摘要：背景：在生成性人工智慧帶來的機遇與風險中，學習研究需要設想隨著人工智慧持續增強或自動化各種任務，人類的思維和責任應如何重新調整。<lb/>

要點：學生和教師作為負責任的智識過程治理者，在人類和人工系統之間分配工作，並受到五個核心原則的指導。具備知識智慧意味著理解知識的演變狀態並採取有目的的行動來推進它。具備智力智慧強調在如何協調分散的認知過程和資源方面做出明智的選擇。具備情境智慧需要敏感地識別機會和風險。具備倫理智慧則強調在使用知識和智力權力時的倫理判斷、責任和關懷。最後，自我與社群成長定義了總體目的，將智識工作與個人發展和集體福祉的提升對齊。<lb/>  
貢獻：這些原則提供了一個視角，以觀察人類思維在人工智慧融入的學習環境中的適應，呼籲發展元層次的性格和能力，這些特徵是智慧導向的、社會負責的知識建構者在人工智慧時代的標誌。

##### **Facts as First Class Objects: Knowledge Objects for Persistent LLM Memory**
2603.17781v1 by Oliver Zahn, Simran Chana

Large language models increasingly serve as persistent knowledge workers, with in-context memory - facts stored in the prompt - as the default strategy. We benchmark in-context memory against Knowledge Objects (KOs), discrete hash-addressed tuples with O(1) retrieval. Within the context window, Claude Sonnet 4.5 achieves 100% exact-match accuracy from 10 to 7,000 facts (97.5% of its 200K window). However, production deployment reveals three failure modes: capacity limits (prompts overflow at 8,000 facts), compaction loss (summarization destroys 60% of facts), and goal drift (cascading compaction erodes 54% of project constraints while the model continues with full confidence). KOs achieve 100% accuracy across all conditions at 252x lower cost. On multi-hop reasoning, KOs reach 78.9% versus 31.6% for in-context. Cross-model replication across four frontier models confirms compaction loss is architectural, not model-specific. We additionally show that embedding retrieval fails on adversarial facts (20% precision at 1) and that neural memory (Titans) stores facts but fails to retrieve them on demand. We introduce density-adaptive retrieval as a switching mechanism and release the benchmark suite.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地作為持久的知識工作者，使用上下文記憶——存儲在提示中的事實——作為默認策略。<lb/>我們將上下文記憶與知識物件（KOs）進行基準測試，KOs 是具有 O(1) 檢索的離散哈希地址元組。<lb/>在上下文窗口內，Claude Sonnet 4.5 從 10 到 7,000 個事實實現了 100% 的精確匹配準確率（其 200K 窗口的 97.5%）。<lb/>然而，生產部署揭示了三種失效模式：容量限制（提示在 8,000 個事實時溢出）、壓縮損失（摘要摧毀了 60% 的事實）和目標漂移（級聯壓縮侵蝕了 54% 的項目約束，而模型仍然充滿信心地繼續）。<lb/>KOs 在所有條件下以 252 倍更低的成本達到 100% 的準確率。<lb/>在多跳推理中，KOs 達到 78.9%，而上下文記憶為 31.6%。<lb/>跨四個前沿模型的跨模型複製確認了壓縮損失是架構性的，而不是特定於模型的。<lb/>我們還顯示嵌入檢索在對抗性事實上失敗（在 1 時的精確度為 20%），並且神經記憶（Titans）儲存事實但未能按需檢索它們。<lb/>我們引入密度自適應檢索作為切換機制並發布基準套件。

##### **Modeling Overlapped Speech with Shuffles**
2603.17769v1 by Matthew Wiesner, Samuele Cornell, Alexander Polok, Lucas Ondel Yang, Lukáš Burget, Sanjeev Khudanpur

We propose to model parallel streams of data, such as overlapped speech, using shuffles. Specifically, this paper shows how the shuffle product and partial order finite-state automata (FSAs) can be used for alignment and speaker-attributed transcription of overlapped speech. We train using the total score on these FSAs as a loss function, marginalizing over all possible serializations of overlapping sequences at subword, word, and phrase levels. To reduce graph size, we impose temporal constraints by constructing partial order FSAs. We address speaker attribution by modeling (token, speaker) tuples directly. Viterbi alignment through the shuffle product FSA directly enables one-pass alignment. We evaluate performance on synthetic LibriSpeech overlaps. To our knowledge, this is the first algorithm that enables single-pass alignment of multi-talker recordings. All algorithms are implemented using k2 / Icefall.

摘要：我們提出使用洗牌來建模平行數據流，例如重疊的語音。具體而言，本文展示了如何使用洗牌乘積和部分有序有限狀態自動機（FSA）來對重疊語音進行對齊和說話者歸屬轉錄。我們使用這些 FSA 的總分作為損失函數，並在子詞、單詞和短語層面上對所有可能的重疊序列進行邊際化。為了減少圖形大小，我們通過構建部分有序 FSA 來施加時間約束。我們通過直接建模（標記、說話者）元組來解決說話者歸屬問題。通過洗牌乘積 FSA 的 Viterbi 對齊直接實現了一次性對齊。我們在合成的 LibriSpeech 重疊上評估性能。據我們所知，這是第一個能夠實現多講者錄音的一次性對齊的算法。所有算法均使用 k2 / Icefall 實現。

##### **Adaptive Guidance for Retrieval-Augmented Masked Diffusion Models**
2603.17677v1 by Jaemin Kim, Jong Chul Ye

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) improves factual grounding by incorporating external knowledge into language model generation. However, when retrieved context is noisy, unreliable, or inconsistent with the model's parametric knowledge, it introduces retrieval-prior conflicts that can degrade generation quality. While this problem has been studied in autoregressive language models, it remains largely unexplored in diffusion-based language models, where the iterative denoising process introduces unique challenges for integrating retrieved context. In this work, we propose Adaptive Retrieval-Augmented Masked Diffusion (ARAM), a training-free adaptive guidance framework for Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs) in RAG settings. ARAM dynamically calibrates the guidance scale during denoising according to the Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SNR) of the distributional shift induced by retrieved context. Intuitively, the model strengthens guidance when the retrieved context provides reliable corrective evidence and suppresses it when the contextual signal is noisy or non-supportive. Extensive experiments on multiple knowledge-intensive QA benchmarks show that ARAM improves overall QA performance over competitive RAG baselines.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）通過將外部知識納入語言模型生成來改善事實基礎。然而，當檢索的上下文嘈雜、不可靠或與模型的參數知識不一致時，會引入檢索優先衝突，從而降低生成質量。雖然這個問題在自回歸語言模型中已經被研究，但在基於擴散的語言模型中仍然很大程度上未被探索，因為迭代去噪過程為整合檢索上下文帶來了獨特的挑戰。在這項工作中，我們提出了自適應檢索增強遮罩擴散（ARAM），這是一個無需訓練的自適應指導框架，適用於RAG設置中的遮罩擴散模型（MDMs）。ARAM根據檢索上下文引起的分佈變化的信噪比（SNR）在去噪過程中動態調整指導比例。直觀上，當檢索的上下文提供可靠的修正證據時，模型會加強指導，而當上下文信號嘈雜或不支持時則會抑制指導。在多個知識密集型問答基準上的大量實驗顯示，ARAM在整體問答性能上優於競爭性的RAG基準。

##### **Training-Only Heterogeneous Image-Patch-Text Graph Supervision for Advancing Few-Shot Learning Adapters**
2603.18101v1 by Mohammed Rahman Sherif Khan Mohammad, Ardhendu Behera, Sandip Pradhan, Swagat Kumar, Amr Ahmed

Recent adapter-based CLIP tuning (e.g., Tip-Adapter) is a strong few-shot learner, achieving efficiency by caching support features for fast prototype matching. However, these methods rely on global uni-modal feature vectors, overlooking fine-grained patch relations and their structural alignment with class text. To bridge this gap without incurring inference costs, we introduce a novel asymmetric training-only framework. Instead of altering the lightweight adapter, we construct a high-capacity auxiliary Heterogeneous Graph Teacher that operates solely during training. This teacher (i) integrates multi-scale visual patches and text prompts into a unified graph, (ii) performs deep cross-modal reasoning via a Modality-aware Graph Transformer (MGT), and (iii) applies discriminative node filtering to extract high-fidelity class features. Crucially, we employ a cache-aware dual-objective strategy to supervise this relational knowledge directly into the Tip-Adapter's key-value cache, effectively upgrading the prototypes while the graph teacher is discarded at test time. Thus, inference remains identical to Tip-Adapter with zero extra latency or memory. Across standard 1-16-shot benchmarks, our method consistently establishes a new state-of-the-art. Ablations confirm that the auxiliary graph supervision, text-guided reasoning, and node filtering are the essential ingredients for robust few-shot adaptation. Code is available at https://github.com/MR-Sherif/TOGA.git.

摘要：最近基於適配器的 CLIP 調整（例如，Tip-Adapter）是一種強大的少量學習者，通過緩存支持特徵來實現快速原型匹配的高效性。<lb/>然而，這些方法依賴於全局單模態特徵向量，忽視了細粒度的補丁關係及其與類別文本的結構對齊。<lb/>為了在不增加推理成本的情況下彌補這一差距，我們引入了一種新穎的非對稱訓練專用框架。<lb/>我們並不改變輕量級的適配器，而是構建了一個高容量的輔助異質圖教師，該教師僅在訓練期間運作。<lb/>這位教師 (i) 將多尺度的視覺補丁和文本提示整合到一個統一的圖中， (ii) 通過一個模態感知圖變換器 (MGT) 執行深度跨模態推理，並 (iii) 應用區分性節點過濾以提取高保真度的類別特徵。<lb/>至關重要的是，我們採用一種緩存感知的雙目標策略，將這種關係知識直接監督到 Tip-Adapter 的鍵值緩存中，有效地升級了原型，同時在測試時丟棄圖教師。<lb/>因此，推理與 Tip-Adapter 保持一致，沒有額外的延遲或內存。<lb/>在標準的 1-16 次拍攝基準中，我們的方法始終建立了新的最先進技術。<lb/>消融實驗證實，輔助圖監督、文本引導推理和節點過濾是穩健少量適應的必要成分。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/MR-Sherif/TOGA.git 獲得。

##### **From Isolated Scoring to Collaborative Ranking: A Comparison-Native Framework for LLM-Based Paper Evaluation**
2603.17588v1 by Pujun Zheng, Jiacheng Yao, Jinquan Zheng, Chenyang Gu, Guoxiu He, Jiawei Liu, Yong Huang, Tianrui Guo, Wei Lu

Large language models (LLMs) are currently applied to scientific paper evaluation by assigning an absolute score to each paper independently. However, since score scales vary across conferences, time periods, and evaluation criteria, models trained on absolute scores are prone to fitting narrow, context-specific rules rather than developing robust scholarly judgment. To overcome this limitation, we propose shifting paper evaluation from isolated scoring to collaborative ranking. In particular, we design \textbf{C}omparison-\textbf{N}ative framework for \textbf{P}aper \textbf{E}valuation (\textbf{CNPE}), integrating comparison into both data construction and model learning. We first propose a graph-based similarity ranking algorithm to facilitate the sampling of more informative and discriminative paper pairs from a collection. We then enhance relative quality judgment through supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning with comparison-based rewards. At inference, the model performs pairwise comparisons over sampled paper pairs and aggregates these preference signals into a global relative quality ranking. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework achieves an average relative improvement of \textbf{21.8\%} over the strong baseline DeepReview-14B, while exhibiting robust generalization to five previously unseen datasets. \href{https://github.com/ECNU-Text-Computing/ComparisonReview}{Code}.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）目前應用於科學論文評估，通過為每篇論文獨立分配絕對分數。然而，由於分數範圍在不同會議、時間段和評估標準之間有所不同，基於絕對分數訓練的模型容易適應狹窄的、特定上下文的規則，而不是發展出穩健的學術判斷。為了克服這一限制，我們建議將論文評估從孤立的打分轉變為協作排名。特別是，我們設計了\textbf{C}omparison-\textbf{N}ative框架，用於\textbf{P}aper \textbf{E}valuation（\textbf{CNPE}），將比較整合到數據構建和模型學習中。我們首先提出了一種基於圖的相似性排名算法，以促進從集合中抽取更具信息性和區分性的論文對。我們然後通過基於比較的獎勵進行監督微調和強化學習，增強相對質量判斷。在推理階段，模型對抽樣的論文對進行成對比較，並將這些偏好信號聚合成一個全局相對質量排名。實驗結果表明，我們的框架在強基準DeepReview-14B上實現了平均相對提升\textbf{21.8\%}，同時對五個之前未見過的數據集展現了穩健的泛化能力。 \href{https://github.com/ECNU-Text-Computing/ComparisonReview}{代碼}。

##### **KA2L: A Knowledge-Aware Active Learning Framework for LLMs**
2603.17566v1 by Haoxuan Yin, Bojian Liu, Chen Tang, Yangfan Wang, Lian Yan, Jingchi Jiang

Fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) with high-quality knowledge has been shown to enhance their performance effectively. However, there is a paucity of research on the depth of domain-specific knowledge comprehension by LLMs and the application of targeted active learning to improve their expertise. To address this gap, we introduce the Knowledge-Aware Active Learning (KA2L) framework. This framework assesses LLMs' mastery of specific knowledge points to aid in constructing unanswerable or unknowable questions through latent space analysis. This active learning strategy enhances training efficiency by focusing on knowledge the model has yet to master, thereby minimizing redundancy in learning already acquired information. This study innovatively employs a knowledge distribution probing technique to examine the hidden states of specific Transformer layers and identify the distribution of known and unknown knowledge within the LLM. Additionally, a hidden-state decoding method is proposed to generate numerous unknown questions in natural language from the latent knowledge space. In our experiments, we selected nine open-source LLMs to validate the effectiveness of the proposed framework. Results indicate that KA2L not only significantly reduces 50% annotation and computation costs across two open-domain and one vertical-domain dataset but also achieves better performance, offering valuable insights into active learning strategies for LLMs. The code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/KA2L-F15C.

摘要：微調大型語言模型（LLMs）以高品質知識已被證明能有效提升其表現。然而，對於LLMs在特定領域知識理解的深度以及針對性主動學習應用以提升其專業知識的研究仍然稀缺。為了解決這一空白，我們引入了知識感知主動學習（KA2L）框架。該框架評估LLMs對特定知識點的掌握程度，以幫助通過潛在空間分析構建無法回答或未知的問題。這種主動學習策略通過專注於模型尚未掌握的知識來提高訓練效率，從而最小化對已獲得信息的學習冗餘。本研究創新性地採用了知識分佈探測技術，以檢查特定Transformer層的隱藏狀態，並識別LLM內已知和未知知識的分佈。此外，提出了一種隱藏狀態解碼方法，從潛在知識空間生成大量自然語言的未知問題。在我們的實驗中，我們選擇了九個開源LLMs來驗證所提出框架的有效性。結果表明，KA2L不僅在兩個開放領域和一個垂直領域數據集上顯著減少了50%的標註和計算成本，還實現了更好的性能，為LLMs的主動學習策略提供了有價值的見解。代碼可在 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/KA2L-F15C 獲得。

##### **Zipper-LoRA: Dynamic Parameter Decoupling for Speech-LLM based Multilingual Speech Recognition**
2603.17558v2 by Yuxiang Mei, Delai Qiu, Shengping Liu, Jiaen Liang, Yanhua Long

Speech Large Language Models (Speech-LLMs) have emerged as a powerful approach for automatic speech recognition (ASR) by aligning speech encoders with large language models. However, adapting these systems to multilingual settings with imbalanced data distributions remains challenging. In such scenarios, a stability-plasticity dilemma often arises: fully shared Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) can cause negative inter-lingual interference for under-represented languages, while fully language-specific tuning limits the cross-lingual beneficial knowledge transfer needed for low-resource tasks. To address this, we propose Zipper-LoRA, a novel rank-level decoupling framework with three variants (Static, Hard, and Soft) that dynamically synthesizes LoRA updates from shared and language-specific subspaces. By using a lightweight language-conditioned router, Zipper-LoRA dynamically controls the contribution of each subspace at the LoRA rank level, enabling fine-grained sharing where languages are compatible and strict decoupling when conflicts occur. To further stabilize optimization under imbalanced data, we propose a two-stage training strategy with an Initial-B warm start that significantly accelerates convergence. Experiments on a 12-language mixed-resource setting show that Zipper-LoRA consistently outperforms both fully shared and independent baselines, particularly in extremely low-resource scenarios. Moreover, we demonstrate that these gains are robust across both chunked and non-chunked encoder configurations, confirming the framework's reliability for practical, large-scale multilingual ASR. Our code and data will be available at https://github.com/YuCeong-May/Zipper-LoRA for reproducibility.

摘要：語音大型語言模型（Speech-LLMs）已成為自動語音識別（ASR）的強大方法，通過將語音編碼器與大型語言模型對齊。然而，將這些系統適應於數據分佈不平衡的多語言環境仍然具有挑戰性。在這種情況下，經常會出現穩定性-可塑性困境：完全共享的參數高效微調（PEFT）可能會對代表性不足的語言造成負面的跨語言干擾，而完全語言特定的調整則限制了低資源任務所需的跨語言有益知識轉移。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了Zipper-LoRA，一種新穎的秩級解耦框架，具有三種變體（靜態、硬性和軟性），能夠動態合成來自共享和語言特定子空間的LoRA更新。通過使用輕量級的語言條件路由器，Zipper-LoRA在LoRA秩級別上動態控制每個子空間的貢獻，實現語言兼容時的細粒度共享，以及在衝突發生時的嚴格解耦。為了進一步穩定不平衡數據下的優化，我們提出了一種兩階段的訓練策略，具有初始-B熱啟動，顯著加速收斂。在12種語言的混合資源設置下的實驗顯示，Zipper-LoRA在極低資源場景中特別超越了完全共享和獨立基準。此外，我們證明這些增益在分塊和非分塊編碼器配置中都是穩健的，確認了該框架在實際大型多語言ASR中的可靠性。我們的代碼和數據將在https://github.com/YuCeong-May/Zipper-LoRA上提供，以便重現。

##### **CLeAN: Continual Learning Adaptive Normalization in Dynamic Environments**
2603.17548v1 by Isabella Marasco, Davide Evangelista, Elena Loli Piccolomini, Michele Colajanni

Artificial intelligence systems predominantly rely on static data distributions, making them ineffective in dynamic real-world environments, such as cybersecurity, autonomous transportation, or finance, where data shifts frequently. Continual learning offers a potential solution by enabling models to learn from sequential data while retaining prior knowledge. However, a critical and underexplored issue in this domain is data normalization. Conventional normalization methods, such as min-max scaling, presuppose access to the entire dataset, which is incongruent with the sequential nature of continual learning. In this paper we introduce Continual Learning Adaptive Normalization (CLeAN), a novel adaptive normalization technique designed for continual learning in tabular data. CLeAN involves the estimation of global feature scales using learnable parameters that are updated via an Exponential Moving Average (EMA) module, enabling the model to adapt to evolving data distributions. Through comprehensive evaluations on two datasets and various continual learning strategies, including Resevoir Experience Replay, A-GEM, and EwC we demonstrate that CLeAN not only improves model performance on new data but also mitigates catastrophic forgetting. The findings underscore the importance of adaptive normalization in enhancing the stability and effectiveness of tabular data, offering a novel perspective on the use of normalization to preserve knowledge in dynamic learning environments.

摘要：人工智慧系統主要依賴靜態數據分佈，使其在動態的現實環境中（例如網絡安全、自主運輸或金融）無法有效運作，因為這些環境中的數據經常變動。持續學習提供了一個潛在的解決方案，通過使模型能夠從序列數據中學習，同時保留先前的知識。然而，在這個領域中，一個關鍵且未被充分探討的問題是數據正規化。傳統的正規化方法，如最小-最大縮放，假設可以訪問整個數據集，這與持續學習的序列特性不相符。在本文中，我們介紹了持續學習自適應正規化（CLeAN），這是一種專為表格數據中的持續學習設計的新型自適應正規化技術。CLeAN 涉及使用可學習參數來估計全局特徵尺度，這些參數通過指數移動平均（EMA）模塊進行更新，使模型能夠適應不斷變化的數據分佈。通過對兩個數據集和各種持續學習策略（包括儲存經驗重播、A-GEM 和 EwC）進行全面評估，我們展示了 CLeAN 不僅提高了模型在新數據上的性能，還減輕了災難性遺忘。研究結果強調了自適應正規化在增強表格數據的穩定性和有效性方面的重要性，並為在動態學習環境中使用正規化以保留知識提供了一種新視角。

##### **Language on Demand, Knowledge at Core: Composing LLMs with Encoder-Decoder Translation Models for Extensible Multilinguality**
2603.17512v1 by Mengyu Bu, Yang Feng

Large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong general intelligence, yet their multilingual performance remains highly imbalanced. Although LLMs encode substantial cross-lingual knowledge in a unified semantic space, they often struggle to reliably interface this knowledge with low-resource or unseen languages. Fortunately, pretrained encoder-decoder translation models already possess balanced multilingual capability, suggesting a natural complement to LLMs. In this work, we propose XBridge, a compositional encoder-LLM-decoder architecture that offloads multilingual understanding and generation to external pretrained translation models, while preserving the LLM as an English-centric core for general knowledge processing. To address the resulting representation misalignment across models, we introduce lightweight cross-model mapping layers and an optimal transport-based alignment objective, enabling fine-grained semantic consistency for multilingual generation. Experiments on four LLMs across multilingual understanding, reasoning, summarization, and generation indicate that XBridge outperforms strong baselines, especially on low-resource and previously unseen languages, without retraining the LLM.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）展現出強大的通用智慧，但它們的多語言表現仍然高度不平衡。儘管LLMs在統一的語義空間中編碼了大量的跨語言知識，但它們在與低資源或未見語言可靠地對接這些知識時經常遇到困難。幸運的是，預訓練的編碼器-解碼器翻譯模型已經具備平衡的多語言能力，這表明它們可以自然地補充LLMs。在本研究中，我們提出了XBridge，一種組合的編碼器-LLM-解碼器架構，將多語言理解和生成的任務轉移到外部預訓練的翻譯模型，同時保留LLM作為以英語為中心的核心，用於一般知識處理。為了解決模型之間的表示不對齊問題，我們引入了輕量級的跨模型映射層和基於最佳運輸的對齊目標，從而實現多語言生成的細粒度語義一致性。在四個LLMs上進行的多語言理解、推理、總結和生成的實驗表明，XBridge在強基準之上表現出色，特別是在低資源和之前未見的語言上，且無需重新訓練LLM。

##### **Inducing Epistemological Humility in Large Language Models: A Targeted SFT Approach to Reducing Hallucination**
2603.17504v1 by Cem Uluoglakci, Tugba Taskaya Temizel

Large language models (LLMs) often hallucinate, producing fluent but false information, partly because supervised fine-tuning (SFT) implicitly rewards always responding. We introduce $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$, an SFT dataset (31,487 responses for 11,151 questions) designed to teach models epistemological humility-the ability to recognize the limits of their own knowledge and admit uncertainty. This is achieved through questions about non-existent "hypothetical" terms. We also release $\textit{HypoTermQA-Enhanced}$, a benchmark for hallucination tendency strengthened through multiple validations. We conducted 800 controlled LoRA SFT runs across $\textit{Llama3.1-8B}$ and $\textit{Gemma3-4B}$ (base and instruct), testing 100 fine-tuning configurations with paired controls. Our results demonstrate that replacing generic instruction data with $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$ significantly improves the HypoTerm Score (median increases of 0.19% to 25.91%) and FactScore (+0.39% to +0.86%), while maintaining stable performance on MMLU (minimal decreases of 0.26% to 0.35%). Our work demonstrates that targeted, high-quality SFT data teaching meta-cognitive skills can effectively reduce hallucination without preference/RL pipelines, providing mechanistic insights and a practical path toward more reliable AI systems.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）經常會出現幻覺，產生流暢但虛假的資訊，部分原因是監督式微調（SFT）隱含地獎勵總是回應。我們介紹了 $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$，這是一個 SFT 數據集（31,487 個回應對應 11,151 個問題），旨在教導模型認識認識論的謙遜——識別自身知識的局限性並承認不確定性。這是通過關於不存在的「假設」術語的問題來實現的。我們還發布了 $\textit{HypoTermQA-Enhanced}$，這是一個通過多次驗證強化的幻覺傾向基準。我們在 $\textit{Llama3.1-8B}$ 和 $\textit{Gemma3-4B}$（基礎和指令）上進行了 800 次控制的 LoRA SFT 執行，測試了 100 種微調配置及其配對控制。我們的結果顯示，用 $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$ 替換通用指令數據顯著提高了 HypoTerm 分數（中位數增加 0.19% 到 25.91%）和 FactScore（+0.39% 到 +0.86%），同時在 MMLU 上保持穩定的表現（最小下降 0.26% 到 0.35%）。我們的工作表明，針對性的高質量 SFT 數據教導元認知技能可以有效減少幻覺，而無需偏好/RL 管道，提供了機制上的見解和通向更可靠 AI 系統的實用途徑。

##### **Revisiting Cross-Attention Mechanisms: Leveraging Beneficial Noise for Domain-Adaptive Learning**
2603.17474v1 by Zelin Zang, Yehui Yang, Fei Wang, Liangyu Li, Baigui Sun

Unsupervised Domain Adaptation (UDA) seeks to transfer knowledge from a labeled source domain to an unlabeled target domain but often suffers from severe domain and scale gaps that degrade performance. Existing cross-attention-based transformers can align features across domains, yet they struggle to preserve content semantics under large appearance and scale variations. To explicitly address these challenges, we introduce the concept of beneficial noise, which regularizes cross-attention by injecting controlled perturbations, encouraging the model to ignore style distractions and focus on content. We propose the Domain-Adaptive Cross-Scale Matching (DACSM) framework, which consists of a Domain-Adaptive Transformer (DAT) for disentangling domain-shared content from domain-specific style, and a Cross-Scale Matching (CSM) module that adaptively aligns features across multiple resolutions. DAT incorporates beneficial noise into cross-attention, enabling progressive domain translation with enhanced robustness, yielding content-consistent and style-invariant representations. Meanwhile, CSM ensures semantic consistency under scale changes. Extensive experiments on VisDA-2017, Office-Home, and DomainNet demonstrate that DACSM achieves state-of-the-art performance, with up to +2.3% improvement over CDTrans on VisDA-2017. Notably, DACSM achieves a +5.9% gain on the challenging "truck" class of VisDA, evidencing the strength of beneficial noise in handling scale discrepancies. These results highlight the effectiveness of combining domain translation, beneficial-noise-enhanced attention, and scale-aware alignment for robust cross-domain representation learning.

摘要：無監督領域適應（UDA）旨在將知識從標記的源領域轉移到未標記的目標領域，但通常會受到嚴重的領域和規模差距的影響，從而降低性能。現有的基於交叉注意力的Transformer可以對齊跨領域的特徵，但在面對大幅外觀和規模變化時，它們難以保持內容語義。為了明確解決這些挑戰，我們引入了有益噪聲的概念，通過注入受控擾動來正則化交叉注意力，鼓勵模型忽略風格干擾，專注於內容。我們提出了領域自適應跨尺度匹配（DACSM）框架，其中包含一個領域自適應Transformer（DAT），用於將領域共享的內容與領域特定的風格解耦，以及一個跨尺度匹配（CSM）模塊，該模塊自適應地對齊多個解析度的特徵。DAT將有益噪聲納入交叉注意力中，使得在增強魯棒性的情況下進行漸進式領域翻譯，產生內容一致且風格不變的表示。同時，CSM確保在規模變化下的語義一致性。在VisDA-2017、Office-Home和DomainNet上的大量實驗表明，DACSM實現了最先進的性能，在VisDA-2017上比CDTrans提高了高達+2.3%。值得注意的是，DACSM在VisDA的挑戰性“卡車”類別上獲得了+5.9%的增益，證明了有益噪聲在處理規模差異方面的優勢。這些結果突顯了結合領域翻譯、有益噪聲增強的注意力和規模感知對齊在穩健的跨領域表示學習中的有效性。

##### **When Only the Final Text Survives: Implicit Execution Tracing for Multi-Agent Attribution**
2603.17445v2 by Yi Nian, Haosen Cao, Shenzhe Zhu, Henry Peng Zou, Qingqing Luan, Yue Zhao

When a multi-agent system produces an incorrect or harmful answer, who is accountable if execution logs and agent identifiers are unavailable? Multi-agent language systems increasingly rely on structured interactions such as delegation and iterative refinement, yet the final output often obscures the underlying interaction topology and agent contributions. We introduce IET (Implicit Execution Tracing), a metadata-independent framework that enables token-level attribution directly from generated text and a simple mechanism for interaction topology reconstruction. During generation, agent-specific keyed signals are embedded into the token distribution, transforming the text into a self-describing execution trace detectable only with a secret key. At detection time, a transition-aware scoring method identifies agent handover points and reconstructs the interaction graph. Experiments show that IET recovers agent segments and coordination structure with high accuracy while preserving generation quality, enabling privacy-preserving auditing for multi-agent language systems.

摘要：當多代理系統產生不正確或有害的答案時，如果執行日誌和代理識別碼不可用，誰應該負責？多代理語言系統越來越依賴於結構化互動，例如授權和迭代精煉，然而最終的輸出往往掩蓋了底層的互動拓撲和代理貢獻。我們介紹了 IET（隱式執行追蹤），這是一個與元數據無關的框架，能夠直接從生成的文本中實現令牌級的歸因，並提供一種簡單的互動拓撲重建機制。在生成過程中，特定於代理的鍵控信號被嵌入到令牌分佈中，將文本轉換為僅能通過秘密密鑰檢測的自描述執行追蹤。在檢測時，基於轉換的評分方法識別代理交接點並重建互動圖。實驗顯示，IET 能夠高精度地恢復代理段和協調結構，同時保持生成質量，實現多代理語言系統的隱私保護審計。

##### **Proactive Knowledge Inquiry in Doctor-Patient Dialogue: Stateful Extraction, Belief Updating, and Path-Aware Action Planning**
2603.17425v1 by Zhenhai Pan, Yan Liu, Jia You

Most automated electronic medical record (EMR) pipelines remain output-oriented: they transcribe, extract, and summarize after the consultation, but they do not explicitly model what is already known, what is still missing, which uncertainty matters most, or what question or recommendation should come next. We formulate doctor-patient dialogue as a proactive knowledge-inquiry problem under partial observability. The proposed framework combines stateful extraction, sequential belief updating, gap-aware state modeling, hybrid retrieval over objectified medical knowledge, and a POMDP-lite action planner. Instead of treating the EMR as the only target artifact, the framework treats documentation as the structured projection of an ongoing inquiry loop. To make the formulation concrete, we report a controlled pilot evaluation on ten standardized multi-turn dialogues together with a 300-query retrieval benchmark aggregated across dialogues. On this pilot protocol, the full framework reaches 83.3% coverage, 80.0% risk recall, 81.4% structural completeness, and lower redundancy than the chunk-only and template-heavy interactive baselines. These pilot results do not establish clinical generalization; rather, they suggest that proactive inquiry may be methodologically interesting under tightly controlled conditions and can be viewed as a conceptually appealing formulation worth further investigation for dialogue-based EMR generation. This work should be read as a pilot concept demonstration under a controlled simulated setting rather than as evidence of clinical deployment readiness. No implication of clinical deployment readiness, clinical safety, or real-world clinical utility should be inferred from this pilot protocol.

摘要：大多數自動化電子病歷 (EMR) 管道仍然以輸出為導向：它們在諮詢後進行轉錄、提取和總結，但並未明確建模已知的內容、仍缺失的內容、最重要的不確定性，或下一步應該提出的問題或建議。我們將醫生-病人對話定義為在部分可觀察性下的主動知識探詢問題。所提出的框架結合了有狀態的提取、序列信念更新、關注差距的狀態建模、對物化醫療知識的混合檢索，以及一個簡化的 POMDP 行動規劃器。該框架並不將 EMR 視為唯一的目標產物，而是將文檔視為持續探詢循環的結構化投影。為了使這一表述具體化，我們報告了對十個標準化的多輪對話進行的受控初步評估，並提供了一個跨對話聚合的 300 查詢檢索基準。在這一初步協議中，完整框架達到了 83.3% 的覆蓋率、80.0% 的風險召回率、81.4% 的結構完整性，且比僅使用片段和模板重的互動基準具有更低的冗餘性。這些初步結果並未建立臨床泛化；相反，它們表明在嚴格控制的條件下，主動探詢可能在方法論上具有趣味，並且可以被視為一種概念上吸引人的表述，值得進一步調查以用於基於對話的 EMR 生成。這項工作應被視為在受控模擬環境下的初步概念示範，而不是臨床部署準備的證據。從這一初步協議中不應推斷出臨床部署準備、臨床安全或現實世界臨床效用的任何暗示。

##### **Efficient Exploration at Scale**
2603.17378v1 by Seyed Mohammad Asghari, Chris Chute, Vikranth Dwaracherla, Xiuyuan Lu, Mehdi Jafarnia, Victor Minden, Zheng Wen, Benjamin Van Roy

We develop an online learning algorithm that dramatically improves the data efficiency of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Our algorithm incrementally updates reward and language models as choice data is received. The reward model is fit to the choice data, while the language model is updated by a variation of reinforce, with reinforcement signals provided by the reward model. Several features enable the efficiency gains: a small affirmative nudge added to each reinforcement signal, an epistemic neural network that models reward uncertainty, and information-directed exploration. With Gemma large language models (LLMs), our algorithm matches the performance of offline RLHF trained on 200K labels using fewer than 20K labels, representing more than a 10x gain in data efficiency. Extrapolating from our results, we expect our algorithm trained on 1M labels to match offline RLHF trained on 1B labels. This represents a 1,000x gain. To our knowledge, these are the first results to demonstrate that such large improvements are possible.

##### **Continually self-improving AI**
2603.18073v1 by Zitong Yang

Modern language model-based AI systems are remarkably powerful, yet their capabilities remain fundamentally capped by their human creators in three key ways. First, although a model's weights can be updated via fine-tuning, acquiring new knowledge from small, specialized corpora after pretraining remains highly data-inefficient. Second, the training of these systems relies heavily on finite, human-generated data from across history. Third, the pipelines used to train AI models are confined by the algorithms that human researchers can discover and explore. This thesis takes a small step toward overcoming these inherent limitations, presenting three chapters aimed at breaking these dependencies to create continually self-improving AI. First, to overcome this data-efficiency barrier in knowledge acquisition, we propose a synthetic data approach that diversifies and amplifies small corpora into rich knowledge representations, enabling a model to effectively update its parameters from limited source material. Second, to reduce reliance on human data, we show that given a fixed amount of such data, the model can self-generate synthetic data to bootstrap its fundamental pretraining capabilities without distillation from any off-the-shelf, instruction-tuned LM. Finally, to transcend human-engineered training paradigms, we demonstrate that by scaling search during test time over the space of algorithms, AI can search over a larger space of learning algorithm configurations than human researchers can explore manually.

摘要：現代基於語言模型的人工智慧系統非常強大，但其能力在三個關鍵方面仍然受到其人類創造者的基本限制。首先，儘管模型的權重可以通過微調進行更新，但在預訓練後從小型專門語料庫獲取新知識仍然非常低效。第二，這些系統的訓練在很大程度上依賴於來自歷史的有限人類生成數據。第三，用於訓練人工智慧模型的流程受到人類研究者能夠發現和探索的算法的限制。本論文邁出了一小步，旨在克服這些固有的限制，提出三個章節，旨在打破這些依賴，以創造持續自我改進的人工智慧。首先，為了克服知識獲取中的數據效率障礙，我們提出了一種合成數據的方法，將小型語料庫多樣化並擴展為豐富的知識表示，使模型能夠有效地從有限的來源材料中更新其參數。第二，為了減少對人類數據的依賴，我們展示了在給定固定數量的此類數據的情況下，模型可以自我生成合成數據，以啟動其基本的預訓練能力，而無需從任何現成的、經過指令調整的語言模型中進行蒸餾。最後，為了超越人類設計的訓練範式，我們演示了通過在測試期間擴大算法空間的搜索，人工智慧可以搜索比人類研究者手動探索的學習算法配置更大的空間。

##### **PACE-RAG: Patient-Aware Contextual and Evidence-based Policy RAG for Clinical Drug Recommendation**
2603.17356v1 by Chaeyoung Huh, Hyunmin Hwang, Jung Hwan Shin, Jinse Park, Jong Chul Ye

Drug recommendation requires a deep understanding of individual patient context, especially for complex conditions like Parkinson's disease. While LLMs possess broad medical knowledge, they fail to capture the subtle nuances of actual prescribing patterns. Existing RAG methods also struggle with these complexities because guideline-based retrieval remains too generic and similar-patient retrieval often replicates majority patterns without accounting for the unique clinical nuances of individual patients. To bridge this gap, we propose PACE-RAG (Patient-Aware Contextual and Evidence-based Policy RAG), a novel framework designed to synthesize individual patient context with the prescribing tendencies of similar cases. By analyzing treatment patterns tailored to specific clinical signals, PACE-RAG identifies optimal prescriptions and generates an explainable clinical summary. Evaluated on a Parkinson's cohort and the MIMIC-IV benchmark using Llama-3.1-8B and Qwen3-8B, PACE-RAG achieved state-of-the-art performance, reaching F1 scores of 80.84% and 47.22%, respectively. These results validate PACE-RAG as a robust, clinically grounded solution for personalized decision support. Our code is available at: https://github.com/ChaeYoungHuh/PACE-RAG.

摘要：藥物推薦需要深入了解個別病人的背景，特別是對於像帕金森病這樣的複雜病症。雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）擁有廣泛的醫學知識，但它們無法捕捉實際處方模式的微妙差異。現有的檢索增強生成（RAG）方法在這些複雜性上也面臨挑戰，因為基於指導方針的檢索仍然過於通用，而類似病人的檢索往往重複大多數模式，卻未考慮到個別病人的獨特臨床細微差異。為了彌補這一空白，我們提出了PACE-RAG（以病人為中心的情境和基於證據的政策RAG），這是一個新穎的框架，旨在將個別病人的背景與類似案例的處方趨勢進行綜合。通過分析針對特定臨床信號的治療模式，PACE-RAG識別最佳處方並生成可解釋的臨床摘要。在帕金森病患者群體和MIMIC-IV基準上使用Llama-3.1-8B和Qwen3-8B進行評估，PACE-RAG達到了最先進的表現，分別達到80.84%和47.22%的F1分數。這些結果驗證了PACE-RAG作為個性化決策支持的穩健、臨床基礎解決方案。我們的代碼可在以下網址獲得：https://github.com/ChaeYoungHuh/PACE-RAG。

##### **A Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework for Ride-Hailing Adjudication**
2603.17328v1 by Weiming Wu, Zi-Jian Cheng, Jie Meng, Peng Zhen, Shan Huang, Qun Li, Guobin Wu, Lan-Zhe Guo

The efficient adjudication of responsibility disputes is pivotal for maintaining marketplace fairness. However, the exponential surge in ride-hailing volume renders manual review intractable, while conventional automated methods lack the reasoning transparency required for quasi-judicial decisions. Although Multimodal LLMs offer a promising paradigm, they fundamentally struggle to bridge the gap between general visual semantics and rigorous evidentiary protocols, often leading to perceptual hallucinations and logical looseness. To address these systemic misalignments, we introduce RideJudge, a Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework. Instead of relying on generic pre-training, we bridge the semantic gap via SynTraj, a synthesis engine that grounds abstract liability concepts into concrete trajectory patterns. To resolve the conflict between massive regulation volume and limited context windows, we propose an Adaptive Context Optimization strategy that distills expert knowledge, coupled with a Chain-of-Adjudication mechanism to enforce active evidentiary inquiry. Furthermore, addressing the inadequacy of sparse binary feedback for complex liability assessment, we implement a novel Ordinal-Sensitive Reinforcement Learning mechanism that calibrates decision boundaries against hierarchical severity. Extensive experiments show that our RideJudge-8B achieves 88.41\% accuracy, surpassing 32B-scale baselines and establishing a new standard for interpretable adjudication.
